## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration is governed by restoring forces (functions of x) and possibly damping forces (functions of v), characteristic of nonlinear oscillator equations of motion.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force plus linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring force with linear damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (cubic restoring force with damping and periodic driving)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping term)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Cubic-quintic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity-dependent damping)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force as in a pendulum)
- Mixed nonlinear terms: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x * v**2 (coupling between position and velocity nonlinearities)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-modulated stiffness)
- General polynomial restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 + c3 * v (polynomial restoring force with damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential well, preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power restoring forces (x**2) → asymmetric potential well, breaking oscillation symmetry
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v → linear energy dissipation or injection (damping/anti-damping)
- Terms like (1 - x**2)*v → amplitude-dependent damping, characteristic of self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles)
- Sinusoidal functions of position sin(c*x) → pendulum-like dynamics with bounded restoring force
- Cosine/sine functions of time → external periodic driving forces or parametric excitation
- Products x*v or x**2*v → nonlinear coupling between position and velocity, energy-dependent damping
- Cubic position terms x**3 → hardening (positive coefficient) or softening (negative coefficient) spring behavior

`c0*sin(t) + c1*v + c2*log(c3*v+1) + c4*v**2*x + c5*v*|v|`
Has log and `v*|v|`. **[NO MATCH]**

Missing `v*exp(-x)`. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidates 44-75: All either have wrong basis functions or are missing `v*exp(-x)`.

Let me quickly verify the remaining ones don't have `v*exp(-x)`:

### Candidate 64:
`c0*exp(c1*sin(c2+c3*t)) + c4 + c5*v**5 + c6*v*exp(c7*x) - x`
Has `v*exp(c7*x)` - if c7 is negative, this gives `v*exp(-x)`. But also has `exp(sin(t))` not `sin(t)`, and `v**5` not `v**3`, and `-x`. **[NO MATCH]**
